131.08947634573|help squadron
131.22137156324|&WSQUADRON
131.22158987513|&WSQUADRON is a command used to form and control a Squadron, or a group of small
131.22177575555|&Wspacecrafts. Each capital class ship has three squadron slots. How many ships
131.2222379041|&Win each slot is purely dependant on the type of capital ship. The squadrons are
131.2224348953|&Wlabeled appropriately as 1, 2 and 3.
131.22259224803|&W 
131.22273248414|&WThe first step is to create your squadron. To do this, simply place small
131.22290485144|&Wspacecrafts into one of your hangars on your capital class ship, and use the
131.2230856269|&Wfollowing command while in the bay with the ships.
131.22325168808|&W 
131.22339072303|&WSYNTAX: Squadron add <Squadron #> <shipname>
131.22355468216|&WSquadron remove <shipname>
131.22369942266|&W 
131.2238348541|&WNow that you have formed your squadrons, it is time to sort them into
131.22400211645|&Wpositions: Outer, Midguard, and Center. Positions are used to organize your
131.22420601435|&Wsquadron into protective layers. Only ships in the outermost layer can be hit
131.22438048369|&Wor targeted, so it may be important to keep your vital ships in the center and
131.22455525333|&Wsurround yourself with your squadrons.
131.22471410751|&W 
131.22485254187|&WSYNTAX: Squadron position <squadron #> <Position #>
131.2250168013|&W 
131.22622097007|&WYou have formed your squadron and set its positions! From the bridge, you'll be
131.22642606913|&Wable to launch, control, and recall your squadrons. Scrambling a squadron
131.2266068446|&Wautomatically opens whatever hangar(s) they are in. To recall your squadrons,
131.22678701948|&Wyou must have the bayspace and hangar(s) open, or else your ships cannot be
131.22702004566|&Wfully recalled! The recall flag is toggle-able, so that if you change your mind
131.22720622635|&Wyou can turn it off and leave them in space.
131.22737318841|&W 
131.22751522627|&WSYNTAX: Squadron scramble <Squadron #>
131.22767618249|&WSquadron recall <Squadron #/all> <on/off>
131.22782752939|&W 
131.22796055851|&WThe squadron AI is more advanced than traditional autopilot AI. Launched
131.22813442726|&Wsquadrons act like the old `scramble` system and act as semi-intelligent groups
131.22830469253|&Wof interceptors.
131.22844853214|&W 
131.22858186155|&WWith the squadron command, you can also control your squadron to just about
131.22875182652|&Wanything you can do as if you were on the ship itself.
131.22891488478|&W 
131.22905572147|&WSYNTAX: squadron nav <Squadron #/all/shipname> <command>
131.2292271879|&W(NOTE) A full list of commands can be found on HELP NAVCOMMANDS
131.22938604209|&W 
131.22951967179|&WSquadron target <Squadron #/all/shipname> <victim/none>
131.22967792538|&W 
131.23127757802|&WIn addition to attacking ships, should you position the squadron over a planet,
131.23148417854|&Wit will be possible to bombard the planet using projectiles. Bombarding can
132.72782843027|&Wperm players, and may have serious repercussions if used flippantly. Use this
132.72809418822|&Wcommand with care.
132.72824463423|&W 
132.72837856422|&WSYNTAX:    squadron bombard <planet>
132.72853651753|&W 
132.72868275948|&WSee Also: NAVCOMMANDS BATTLEGROUP FLEETRADAR
132.7288476195|&C---

565.94157499268|help aconfig
566.2615181295|&WACONFIG
566.26174514984|&C[:: &zLegend of the Jedi &C::]
566.26190910897|
566.2620490448|&GSyntax: &Waconfig +/-<option>
566.26220579694|
566.26234122839|&WThis command allows you to configure the actions of your ship while on
566.26250939161|&Wautopilot and unmanned. Typing 'ACONFIG' by itself shows you the 
566.26269467144|&Wcurrent settings. Placing a '+' or '-' next to an option will turn it 
566.26288025157|&Won or off, respectively.
566.26303430108|
566.26317063341|&WThe options are:
566.26331116981|
566.26344299776|&W[ sentinel    ] Move about when on autopilot.
566.26363248168|&W[ autotractor ] Use tractor beams to capture ships in a fight.
566.26380605015|&W[ pirate      ] Attack the pirate threats in a system.
566.26397511424|&W[ autoshield  ] Raise shields when attacked.
566.26413847279|&W[ nocapture   ] Engage self-destruct when captured by tractor beam.
566.26431414331|&W[ usechaff    ] Use chaff when a missile is detected.
566.2644901141|&W[ uselaser    ] Use lasers or ions primarily during combat.
566.2646621811|&W[ uselauncher ] Use projectiles during combat.
566.26483064462|&W[ nointercept ] Scramble interceptors when attacked.
566.26499820725|&W[ clanpost    ] Attack ships owned by enemy clans or clans at war with you.
566.26617444892|&W[ radio       ] Request help from nearby clan ships when attacked.
566.26637234099|&C---

784.50780998036|help squadron
784.79333190795|&WSQUADRON
784.79355592538|&WSQUADRON is a command used to form and control a Squadron, or a group of small
784.79374120521|&Wspacecrafts. Each capital class ship has three squadron slots. How many ships
784.79392198067|&Win each slot is purely dependant on the type of capital ship. The squadrons are
784.79409825176|&Wlabeled appropriately as 1, 2 and 3.
784.79425410302|&W 
784.79439403885|&WThe first step is to create your squadron. To do this, simply place small
784.79456340324|&Wspacecrafts into one of your hangars on your capital class ship, and use the
784.79473607082|&Wfollowing command while in the bay with the ships.
784.7948985285|&W 
784.79503516112|&WSYNTAX: Squadron add <Squadron #> <shipname>
784.79519581706|&WSquadron remove <shipname>
784.79533905609|&W 
784.79547508812|&WNow that you have formed your squadrons, it is time to sort them into
784.79564295104|&Wpositions: Outer, Midguard, and Center. Positions are used to organize your
784.79583363612|&Wsquadron into protective layers. Only ships in the outermost layer can be hit
784.79600960691|&Wor targeted, so it may be important to keep your vital ships in the center and
784.79618317538|&Wsurround yourself with your squadrons.
784.7963408284|&W 
784.79647926276|&WSYNTAX: Squadron position <squadron #> <Position #>
784.79664352219|&W 
784.79791765887|&WYou have formed your squadron and set its positions! From the bridge, you'll be
784.79812756261|&Wable to launch, control, and recall your squadrons. Scrambling a squadron
784.79831194156|&Wautomatically opens whatever hangar(s) they are in. To recall your squadrons,
784.79854797065|&Wyou must have the bayspace and hangar(s) open, or else your ships cannot be
784.79873415137|&Wfully recalled! The recall flag is toggle-able, so that if you change your mind
784.79891462653|&Wyou can turn it off and leave them in space.
784.79907678392|&W 
784.79921702003|&WSYNTAX: Squadron scramble <Squadron #>
784.79938097917|&WSquadron recall <Squadron #/all> <on/off>
784.79953412781|&W 
784.79967466422|&WThe squadron AI is more advanced than traditional autopilot AI. Launched
784.79984372831|&Wsquadrons act like the old `scramble` system and act as semi-intelligent groups
784.80001099066|&Wof interceptors.
784.80015513056|&W 
784.80028966114|&WWith the squadron command, you can also control your squadron to just about
784.80045932581|&Wanything you can do as if you were on the ship itself.
784.80062478641|&W 
784.80076742485|&WSYNTAX: squadron nav <Squadron #/all/shipname> <command>
784.80093979216|&W(NOTE) A full list of commands can be found on HELP NAVCOMMANDS
784.80109924692|&W 
784.80123557925|&WSquadron target <Squadron #/all/shipname> <victim/none>
784.80139383285|&W 
784.80299108314|&WIn addition to attacking ships, should you position the squadron over a planet,
784.80320188774|&Wit will be possible to bombard the planet using projectiles. Bombarding can
784.80338416467|&Wperm players, and may have serious repercussions if used flippantly. Use this
784.80356343866|&Wcommand with care.
784.80371058149|&W 
784.80527089593|&WSYNTAX:    squadron bombard <planet>
784.80546398334|&W 
793.80044671358|&WSee Also: NAVCOMMANDS BATTLEGROUP FLEETRADAR
